pm_dragline_excavators_coal_mine = {
	texture = "gfx/interface/icons/production_method_icons/assembly_lines.dds"
		
	unlocking_technologies = {
		advanced_materials
	}
	
	unlocking_production_methods = {
		pm_diesel_pump_building_coal_mine
		pm_high_pressure_hydraulic_pump_building_coal_mine
		pm_continuous_miners_building_coal_mine
		pm_smart_miners_building_coal_mine
	}

	state_modifiers = {
		workforce_scaled = {
			state_pollution_generation_add = 20
		}
	}
		
	building_modifiers = {
		workforce_scaled = {
			# Input goods
			goods_input_tools_add = 40                           # Price:   40, Total cost: 1600.0
			goods_input_engines_add = 25                         # Price:   60, Total cost: 1500.0
			goods_input_transportation_add = 10                  # Price:   30, Total cost: 300.0
			goods_input_oil_add = 5                              # Price:   40, Total cost: 200.0
			# Output goods
			goods_output_coal_add = 60                           # Price:   30, Total cost: 1800.0
			# Total input cost: 3600.0
			# Total output cost: 1800.0
			# Profit: -1800.0
			# Profit margin: -50.00%
			# Zero profit price multiplier: 2.00
			# Employment: -2000
			# Wage breakeven: 0.90
		}

		level_scaled = {
			building_employment_laborers_add = -1000
			building_employment_machinists_add = -750
			building_employment_engineers_add = -250
		}
	}
}
